<div id="review_1532274506" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1532274506" />
    <a title="Suzanne" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11889829-suzanne"><img alt="Suzanne" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1593566451p2/11889829.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1532274506?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Suzanne" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Suzanne" href="/user/show/11889829-suzanne">Suzanne</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781910751763" href="/book/show/29470014-the-girl-in-the-ice">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11889829-suzanne?shelf=overdrive-browser">overdrive-browser</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11889829-suzanne?shelf=library-wsu">library-wsu</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1532274506" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14138032266113898479">This was a great little book, one I'm glad to have stumbled across. Erika our detective is crumbling, her personal life is a mess (does she have one at all?) her husband Mark was killed at work which just happened to be one of her cases; life at work is not much better. Her first job back after trying to recover from this is just not going well, iniitially Erika is not even able to hold together an initial interview with the parents of a young murdered socialite. <br/><br/>Erika knows she can do it, she's</span>
  <span id="freeText14138032266113898479" style="display:none">This was a great little book, one I'm glad to have stumbled across. Erika our detective is crumbling, her personal life is a mess (does she have one at all?) her husband Mark was killed at work which just happened to be one of her cases; life at work is not much better. Her first job back after trying to recover from this is just not going well, iniitially Erika is not even able to hold together an initial interview with the parents of a young murdered socialite. <br /><br />Erika knows she can do it, she's smarter than this, and the story we see unfolding is as much as a desperate attempt of sorting herself out, as it is finding a warped serial killer. I do look forward to reading Erika's story, the growth she must continue to carry out to try and keep her life from falling apart. <br /><br />I enjoyed watching her become stronger and look forward to what is in store for her character. The author asked for feedback at the end of the novel as to where her development should go. It's too late for me as the second has already been written, but I'd like to see Erika get some spark for life back, ditch those cigarettes, build her reputation and find some looove! I just checked, it seems I'm late the party. He is already up to #5!</span>
  <a data-text-id="14138032266113898479" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1764853320" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1764853320" />
    <a title="Liz" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4125660-liz"><img alt="Liz" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1316269997p2/4125660.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1764853320?book_show_action=true">Dec 27, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Liz" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Liz" href="/user/show/4125660-liz">Liz</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1764853320" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9209883460881685352">4.5 stars<br/><br/>I think this may be my new favorite series. I love Erika Foster. How could I not, with this description of her: “Erika has never quite mastered how to talk to children. Rapists and murderers she could deal with, but children she found a little intimidating.” <br/><br/>This is a fast paced mystery. Well written, with interesting characters. Erika has a nice blend of strength and foibles. She lost her husband, a fellow policeman, in a shootout. She's back in her first job since and still raw. She’s</span>
  <span id="freeText9209883460881685352" style="display:none">4.5 stars<br /><br />I think this may be my new favorite series. I love Erika Foster. How could I not, with this description of her: “Erika has never quite mastered how to talk to children. Rapists and murderers she could deal with, but children she found a little intimidating.” <br /><br />This is a fast paced mystery. Well written, with interesting characters. Erika has a nice blend of strength and foibles. She lost her husband, a fellow policeman, in a shootout. She's back in her first job since and still raw. She’s learning the ins and outs of her new crew. There's competition with another DCI over how to manage the case. In fact, one of the author’s strengths is his detailing of police politics and the kowtowing to the aristocracy. <br />My thanks to all my GR friends that alerted me to this book. All the positive reviews are spot on. The good news is that by discovering this book so long after it was written, I can immediately latch onto the next two in the series. <br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="9209883460881685352" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1827511486?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brenda - Traveling Sisters Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brenda - Traveling Sisters Book Reviews" href="/user/show/10841164-brenda---traveling-sisters-book-reviews">Brenda - Traveling Sisters Book Reviews</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback 9781910751770" href="/book/show/28721136-the-girl-in-the-ice">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1827511486" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1162608125243795772">My sister Norma and I read The Girl in the Ice at the same time so we could share our thoughts on it. You might notice our reviews have some similar thoughts. <br/><br/>The Girl In The Ice is an engaging and suspenseful story that had me hooked right from the Prologue. I found DCI Erika Foster to be a believable, strong and sympathetic character. <br/><br/>I like how the action starts right away and the danger increases as the clock is ticking. I liked how DCI Erika Foster's backstory caused conflict and motivated </span>
  <span id="freeText1162608125243795772" style="display:none">My sister Norma and I read The Girl in the Ice at the same time so we could share our thoughts on it. You might notice our reviews have some similar thoughts. <br /><br />The Girl In The Ice is an engaging and suspenseful story that had me hooked right from the Prologue. I found DCI Erika Foster to be a believable, strong and sympathetic character. <br /><br />I like how the action starts right away and the danger increases as the clock is ticking. I liked how DCI Erika Foster's backstory caused conflict and motivated her to do what it takes to catch the killer and how we are given a glimpse in the head of the villain, that built up more tension for me.<br /><br />I love when a book hooks me right away and slowly reveals layers of clues that draws me into the suspense and tension. I am really forward to more from a strong and likable character. That is what Robert Bryndza has done for me with The Girl In The Ice.<br /><br /><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twogirlslostinacouleereading.wordpress.com/">https://twogirlslostinacouleereading....</a><br /><br /></span>

          </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nnXz8LkH22Dg49GBQtitxSpinO+HvGhfUHDEg1ziW5MBD00OEAU4zOdCvnYgBLW+etH8yKZaIKH1srUhjzR/nA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('2V972YLyfzAb0MXeBefhEfchlXGx4dMA7+IrT7nYATxGJcUnK/CcnBxxqilnO/lqp5L1VpAHm/5KIFrtag4lMw==')})
  }

      <div id="aboutAuthor" class=" clearFloats bigBox"><div class="h2Container gradientHeaderContainer"><h2 class="brownBackground"><a href="/author/show/5763380.Robert_Bryndza">About Robert Bryndza</a></h2></div><div class="bigBoxBody"><div class="bigBoxContent containerWithHeaderContent">
          <div class='bookAuthorProfile'>

<div class='bookAuthorProfile__about'>

<span id="freeTextContainer12940153366392228408">Robert Bryndza is an international bestselling author, best known for his page-turning crime and thriller novels, which have sold over four million copies in the English language.<br/><br/>His crime debut, The Girl in the Ice was released in February 2016, introducing Detective Chief Inspector Erika Foster. Within five months it sold one million copies, reaching number one in the Amazon UK, USA and Australi</span>
  <span id="freeText12940153366392228408" style="display:none">Robert Bryndza is an international bestselling author, best known for his page-turning crime and thriller novels, which have sold over four million copies in the English language.<br /><br />His crime debut, The Girl in the Ice was released in February 2016, introducing Detective Chief Inspector Erika Foster. Within five months it sold one million copies, reaching number one in the Amazon UK, USA and Australian charts. To date, The Girl in the Ice has sold over 1.5 million copies in the English language and has been sold into translation in 29 countries. It was nominated for the Goodreads Choice Award for Mystery &amp; Thriller (2016), the Grand prix des lectrices de Elle in France (2018), and it won two reader voted awards, The Thrillzone Awards best debut thriller in The Netherlands (2018) and The Dead Good Papercut Award for best page turner at the Harrogate Crime Festival (2016).<br /><br />Robert has released a further five novels in the Erika Foster series, The Night Stalker, Dark Water, Last Breath, Cold Blood and Deadly Secrets, all of which have been global bestsellers, and in 2017 Last Breath was a Goodreads Choice Award nominee for Mystery and Thriller.<br /><br />Most recently, Robert created a new crime thriller series based around the central character Kate Marshall, a police officer turned private detective. The first book, Nine Elms, was an Amazon USA #1 bestseller and an Amazon UK top five bestseller, and the series has been sold into translation in 15 countries. The second book, Shadow Sands will be published November 3rd 2020.<br /><br />Robert was born in Lowestoft, on the east coast of England. He studied at Aberystwyth University, and the Guildford School of Acting, and was an actor for several years, but didn’t find success until he took a play he’d written to the Edinburgh Festival. This led to the decision to change career and start writing. He self-published a bestselling series of romantic comedy novels, before switching to writing crime. Robert lives with his husband in Slovakia, and is lucky enough to write full-time.<br /><br />You can find out more about Robert and his books at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.robertbryndza.com">www.robertbryndza.com</a></span>
  <a data-text-id="12940153366392228408" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>
